<Z>Late <C> Slightly, because of the weather issues. I've waited for Wednesday's post and will run into the evening.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>BT/Yahoo <C> Looks like BT/Yahoo are going through one of those phases where they randomly sit on game reports, and either<L.31.1>
release them slowly, or never at all. Can I recommend you make sure that both danny@pbmsports.com and danny.mcconnell@virgin.net<L.31.1>
(my broadband account) are set as trusted addresses, and if you've not had game reports by the next morning, let me know, but also<L.31.1>
lodge a complaint with Yahoo - someone did this last week and they released his reports within hours!<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Deadlines <C> Please keep a note of deadlines over the next few months. I've started doing some work (got to pay the bills) for<L.31.1>
the Football Association (explaining to grassroots leagues how bits of admin software work) and it'll mean I'm out of the office<L.31.1>
quite regularly, especially late afternoon/evenings (one of the reasons I need to crack on with running games in the morning).<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
At present we'll stick with games running on Wednesday and Thursday (but keep an eye on www.pbmsports.com for news about late<L.31.1>
running) but I might decide that moving you to Fridays might offer the most reliable service, not least because that evening I'm<L.31.1>
rarely out at a football function, so there's scope for catching up then if required (which isn't the end of the world for the<L.31.1>
majority playing by email). I'll see how things go, but I want to try and keep running games as promptly as possible.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Processing - 9am <C> See above, from now onwards I'm going to be strict about running games from 9am onwards, as I need to<L.31.1>
crack on with running games. So for those who do still rely on the Royal Snail, please make sure you post orders in time.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Gameplan Baseball <C> The newsletter with a host of discussion points and possible developments for Gameplan Baseball is still<L.31.1>
available, and I'm keen for comments. Those of you playing by post should have had a copy, those by email can download it from<L.31.1>
www.pbmsports.com via the Rules and Newsletters link. Comments are more than welcome. There's a whole host of possibilities, and<L.31.1>
I'm not suggesting all of them will come in now, or indeed at all, but feedback on any or all is welcome.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Late Email Results <C> If you think results are late, please make sure you wait until the following morning before chasing up<L.31.1>
results. First step is to check out the Latest News at www.pbmsports.com - if I am running late I'll post a notice there. Please<L.31.1>
don't chase me up because you know your mate got his half an hour ago, because whilst most emails are "instant", often they do get<L.31.1>
delayed for a few hours and it does take a while to send them all out (I spread them out to avoid triggering firewalls).<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
Equally however, if it's the next morning and you've not had results, and there's nothing on www.pbmsports.com saying I've had a<L.31.1>
problem, then please chase me up. If it hasn't shown 12 hours later, odds are it won't, and probably some firewall or spam filter<L.31.1>
somewhere has gobbled it (and they do appear to do so without pattern). I'd rather you ended up with two copies than none.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>PDF Reports <C> Emailed game reports are available for all games here. The standard format is a PDF file - Adobe Reader is free<L.31.1>
to download (see www.pbmsports.com for a link) and you can open your reports with one click of the mouse and you can either view<L.31.1>
them on screen, or print them as you wish. You don't need to worry about formatting or printer drivers. The text format for<L.31.1>
reports is available but I only expect people will want to do so if they use the text file for other purposes (such as exporting<L.1.1>
<P>
<L>
<L.1.1>
the listings into software produced yourself). If you've not tried email reports before, try them out - it really is very easy.<L.31.1>
